# Tic-tac-toe in Markdown

Play [Tic-tac-toe](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tic-tac-toe) (noughts and crosses) right here in Markdown by clicking on the empty (⬜) squares. Start with the board at the top, or try skipping around if you want. If the links don't work, try reloading the page. Enjoy!
